const generateUniqueId = async ()=>{
    let attempts = 0;
    while(attempts < 10){
        const candidateId = "EXH-".concat(Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000));
        const q = query(collection(db, "users"), where("studentId", "==", candidateId));
        const snap = await getDocs(q);
        if (snap.empty) {
            return candidateId;
        }
        attempts++;
    }
    return "EXH-".concat(Date.now().toString().slice(-6), "-").concat(Math.floor(Math.random() * 100));
};

    const handleAICoreAction = async function(type, target, parentId) {
        let isMastery = arguments.length > 3 && arguments[3] !== void 0 ? arguments[3] : false, overrideSubject = arguments.length > 4 ? arguments[4] : void 0;
        setAILoadingType(type === "quiz" ? "test" : type);
        setShowAILoading(true);
        const taskId = Math.random().toString(36);
        activeAICoreTaskRef.current = taskId;
        try {
            if (type === "notes") {
                var _parentId_match, _parentId_match1, _parentId_match2;
                const classRaw = parentId === null || parentId === void 0 ? void 0 : (_parentId_match = parentId.match(/classes_class_(\d+)/)) === null || _parentId_match === void 0 ? void 0 : _parentId_match[1];
                const clsName = classRaw ? "Class ".concat(classRaw) : (userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.cls) || "Class 12";
                const subRaw = parentId === null || parentId === void 0 ? void 0 : (_parentId_match1 = parentId.match(/subjects_([a-z0-9_]+?)(?:__|$)/)) === null || _parentId_match1 === void 0 ? void 0 : _parentId_match1[1];
                const subName = overrideSubject || (subRaw ? subRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : "General");
                const chapRaw = parentId === null || parentId === void 0 ? void 0 : (_parentId_match2 = parentId.match(/chapters_([a-z0-9_]+?)(?:__|$)/)) === null || _parentId_match2 === void 0 ? void 0 : _parentId_match2[1];
                const chapName = chapRaw ? chapRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : target;
                // Instant local storage cache check
                if ("object" !== "undefined") {
                    const cacheKey = "achivox_notes_full_".concat(subName || "gen", "_").concat(chapName || "none", "_").concat(target || "none", "_").concat((userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id) || "guest").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, "_");
                    try {
                        const cached = localStorage.getItem(cacheKey);
                        if (cached) {
                            const parsed = JSON.parse(cached);
                            if (parsed && parsed.topics) {
                                setShowAILoading(false);
                                setActiveNotes({
                                    title: target,
                                    chapter: chapName,
                                    subjectContext: subName,
                                    classContext: clsName,
                                    mode: "full",
                                    data: parsed
                                });
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                        console.warn("Local cache check failed:", e);
                    }
                }
                if (!(userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.isSubscribed)) {
                    const { allowed } = await checkAndIncrementUsage(userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id, "Smart Notes", 1, target);
                    if (!allowed) {
                        setShowAILoading(false);
                        setShowSubscriptionModal(true);
                        return;
                    }
                }
                const notes = await fetchChapterNotes(target, userData, "dual", subName, chapName);
                if (activeAICoreTaskRef.current !== taskId) return; // Task was cancelled
                if (notes) {
                    setActiveNotes({
                        title: target,
                        chapter: chapName,
                        subjectContext: subName,
                        classContext: clsName,
                        data: notes // Pass fetched data
                    });
                    trackTopicOpen({
                        topicId: target.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "-"),
                        topicName: target,
                        subject: subName,
                        chapter: chapName,
                        cls: clsName,
                        board: (userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.board) || "CBSE"
                    });
                }
            } else if (type === "test" || type === "quiz") {
                // Dashboard Analysis for Test
                const weakAreas = getWeakAreas();
                let finalTarget = target;
                let subjectContext = "";
                if (target === "Daily Challenge" || !target) {
                    if (weakAreas.length > 0) {
                        finalTarget = weakAreas[0].topic;
                        subjectContext = weakAreas[0].subject;
                    } else {
                        finalTarget = "General Science & Logic"; // Default fallback
                    }
                } else if (parentId) {
                    // Check if parentId is actually a subject name (from MasteryRoadmap)
                    if (!parentId.includes("_")) {
                        subjectContext = parentId;
                    } else {
                        var _parentId_match3;
                        const subRaw = parentId === null || parentId === void 0 ? void 0 : (_parentId_match3 = parentId.match(/subjects_([a-z0-9_]+?)(?:__|$)/)) === null || _parentId_match3 === void 0 ? void 0 : _parentId_match3[1];
                        subjectContext = subRaw ? subRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : "General";
                    }
                }
                const questions = await fetchQuestions("full", finalTarget, userData, subjectContext);
                if (activeAICoreTaskRef.current !== taskId) return; // Task was cancelled
                if (questions && questions.length > 0) {
                    setActiveTest({
                        title: finalTarget,
                        subTitle: subjectContext ? "Context: ".concat(subjectContext) : "Practice Test",
                        questions,
                        isMastery,
                        subject: subjectContext || "General",
                        mode: mode
                    });
                } else {
                    alert("AI core was unable to generate questions for this specific topic. Please try a different topic or board.");
                }
            }
        } catch (err) {
            console.error("AI Action Error:", err);
            alert("AI Neural Core connection timeout. Please check your network.");
        } finally{
            setShowAILoading(false);
        }
    };

    // Real-time dynamic performance analyzer for Glowing recommended prep cards
    const getGlowRecommendations = useCallback(()=>{
        const recommends = {
            revisionVault: false,
            flashcards: false,
            timetable: false,
            quickStudy: false,
            battle: false,
            scanSolve: false,
            roadmap: false
        };
        if (!userData) return recommends;
        const totalSolved = userData.totalSolved || 0;
        const correctAnswers = userData.correctAnswers || 0;
        const accuracy = totalSolved > 0 ? correctAnswers / totalSolved * 100 : 100;
        const attempts = userData.attempts || [];
        // 1. Low accuracy (< 70%) or high attempts with failures -> review mistakes
        if (accuracy < 70 || attempts.length > 0 && attempts.some((a)=>a.score < 60)) {
            recommends.revisionVault = true;
            recommends.flashcards = true;
        }
        // 2. Active but weak spots -> Skill roadmap
        if (totalSolved > 15 && accuracy < 85) {
            recommends.roadmap = true;
        }
        // 3. Low study engagement -> AI Timetable Planner
        if ((userData.streak || 0) === 0 || (userData.points || 0) < 1500) {
            recommends.timetable = true;
        }
        // 4. Brand new user -> Quick Study Swipe Cards & Battle Quiz
        if (totalSolved < 5) {
            recommends.quickStudy = true;
            recommends.battle = true;
        }
        // 5. Hard doubts solver -> Scan Camera
        if (attempts.length > 8) {
            recommends.scanSolve = true;
        }
        return recommends;

½webpack/lib/util/registerExternalSerializerØwebpack-sources/ReplaceSourcet  /* __next_internal_client_entry_do_not_use__ sanitizeMathContent,default auto */ import { jsx as _jsx } from "react/jsx-runtime";
import ReactMarkdown from "react-markdown";
import remarkMath from "remark-math";
import rehypeKatex from "rehype-katex";
import "katex/dist/katex.min.css";
export function sanitizeMathContent(content) {
    if (!content) return "";
    // 1. Replace literal "\n" strings with actual newlines
    let processed = content.replace(/\\n/g, "\n");
    // 2. Standardize delimiters: \[ ... \] -> $$ ... $$, \( ... \) -> $ ... $
    processed = processed.replace(/\\\[([\s\S]*?)\\\]/g, "$$$$\n$1\n$$$$");
    processed = processed.replace(/\\\(([\s\S]*?)\\\)/g, "$$$1$$");
    // 3. Extract existing math blocks to prevent double processing
    const mathBlocks = [];
    // Match $$...$$ blocks
    processed = processed.replace(/\$\$([\s\S]*?)\$\$/g, (match)=>{
        mathBlocks.push(match);
        return "__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_".concat(mathBlocks.length - 1, "__");
    });
    // Match $...$ blocks
    processed = processed.replace(/\$([^$]+?)\$/g, (match)=>{
        mathBlocks.push(match);
        return "__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_".concat(mathBlocks.length - 1, "__");
    });
    // 4. Now process non-math text to find raw LaTeX fractions or symbols and wrap them in $
    // Match raw LaTeX fractions (including dfrac and frac with nested braces, up to 1 level for safety):
    const fractionRegex = /\\(d?frac)\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/g;
    processed = processed.replace(fractionRegex, (match)=>{
        return "$".concat(match, "$");
    });
    // Match raw square roots:
    const sqrtRegex = /\\sqrt\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/g;
    processed = processed.replace(sqrtRegex, (match)=>{
        return "$".concat(match, "$");
    });
    // Match common greek letters and math symbols:
    const symbolRegex = /\\(alpha|beta|gamma|delta|theta|pi|mu|sigma|omega|phi|lambda|Delta|pm|times|div|ge|le|ne|approx|infty|degree|cdot)/g;
    processed = processed.replace(symbolRegex, (match)=>{
        return "$".concat(match, "$");
    });
    // 5. Restore the original math blocks
    processed = processed.replace(/__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_(\d+)__/g, (match, index)=>{
        return mathBlocks[parseInt(index, 10)];
    });
    return processed;
}
export default function MathRenderer(param) {
    let { content } = param;
    let safeContent = "";
    if (typeof content === "string") {
        safeContent = content;
    } else if (content && typeof content === "object") {
        // @ts-ignore
        safeContent = content.text || content.en || content.content || JSON.stringify(content);
    }
    if (!safeContent) return null;
    const sanitizedContent = sanitizeMathContent(safeContent);
    return /*#__PURE__*/ _jsx("div", {
        className: "math-rendered w-full overflow-x-auto [&>p]:m-0 [&_.math-display]:my-4 [&_.math-display]:py-1",
        children: /*#__PURE__*/ _jsx(ReactMarkdown, {
            remarkPlugins: [
                remarkMath
            ],
            rehypePlugins: [
                rehypeKatex
            ],
            children: sanitizedContent
        })
    });
}

function sanitizeMathContent(content) {
    if (!content) return "";
    // 1. Replace literal "\n" strings with actual newlines
    let processed = content.replace(/\\n/g, "\n");
    // 2. Standardize delimiters: \[ ... \] -> $$ ... $$, \( ... \) -> $ ... $
    processed = processed.replace(/\\\[([\s\S]*?)\\\]/g, "$$$$\n$1\n$$$$");
    processed = processed.replace(/\\\(([\s\S]*?)\\\)/g, "$$$1$$");
    // 3. Extract existing math blocks to prevent double processing
    const mathBlocks = [];
    // Match $$...$$ blocks
    processed = processed.replace(/\$\$([\s\S]*?)\$\$/g, (match)=>{
        mathBlocks.push(match);
        return "__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_".concat(mathBlocks.length - 1, "__");
    });
    // Match $...$ blocks
    processed = processed.replace(/\$([^$]+?)\$/g, (match)=>{
        mathBlocks.push(match);
        return "__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_".concat(mathBlocks.length - 1, "__");
    });
    // 4. Now process non-math text to find raw LaTeX fractions or symbols and wrap them in $
    // Match raw LaTeX fractions (including dfrac and frac with nested braces, up to 1 level for safety):
    const fractionRegex = /\\(d?frac)\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/g;
    processed = processed.replace(fractionRegex, (match)=>{
        return "$".concat(match, "$");
    });
    // Match raw square roots:
    const sqrtRegex = /\\sqrt\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/g;
    processed = processed.replace(sqrtRegex, (match)=>{
        return "$".concat(match, "$");
    });
    // Match common greek letters and math symbols:
    const symbolRegex = /\\(alpha|beta|gamma|delta|theta|pi|mu|sigma|omega|phi|lambda|Delta|pm|times|div|ge|le|ne|approx|infty|degree|cdot)/g;
    processed = processed.replace(symbolRegex, (match)=>{
        return "$".concat(match, "$");
    });
    // 5. Restore the original math blocks
    processed = processed.replace(/__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_(\d+)__/g, (match, index)=>{
        return mathBlocks[parseInt(index, 10)];
    });
    return processed;
}
function MathRenderer(param) {
    let { content } = param;
    let safeContent = "";
    if (typeof content === "string") {
        safeContent = content;
    } else if (content && typeof content === "object") {
        // @ts-ignore
        safeContent = content.text || content.en || content.content || JSON.stringify(content);
    }
    if (!safeContent) return null;
    const sanitizedContent = sanitizeMathContent(safeContent);
    return /*#__PURE__*/ (0,react_jsx_runtime__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_0__.jsx)("div", {

            rehypePlugins: [
                rehype_katex__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_4__/* ["default"] */ .Z
            ],
            children: sanitizedContent
        })
    });
}

export function sanitizeMathContent(content) {
    if (!content) return "";
    // 1. Replace literal "\n" strings with actual newlines
    let processed = content.replace(/\\n/g, "\n");
    // 2. Standardize delimiters: \[ ... \] -> $$ ... $$, \( ... \) -> $ ... $

        mathBlocks.push(match);
        return "__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_".concat(mathBlocks.length - 1, "__");
    });
    // Match $...$ blocks
    processed = processed.replace(/\$([^$]+?)\$/g, (match)=>{
        mathBlocks.push(match);
        return "__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_".concat(mathBlocks.length - 1, "__");
    });
    // 4. Now process non-math text to find raw LaTeX fractions or symbols and wrap them in $
    // Match raw LaTeX fractions (including dfrac and frac with nested braces, up to 1 level for safety):
    const fractionRegex = /\\(d?frac)\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/g;
    processed = processed.replace(fractionRegex, (match)=>{
        return "$".concat(match, "$");
    });
    // Match raw square roots:
    const sqrtRegex = /\\sqrt\{((?:[^{}]+|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/g;
    processed = processed.replace(sqrtRegex, (match)=>{
        return "$".concat(match, "$");
    });
    // Match common greek letters and math symbols:
    const symbolRegex = /\\(alpha|beta|gamma|delta|theta|pi|mu|sigma|omega|phi|lambda|Delta|pm|times|div|ge|le|ne|approx|infty|degree|cdot)/g;
    processed = processed.replace(symbolRegex, (match)=>{

    processed = processed.replace(/__MATH_BLOCK_PLACEHOLDER_(\d+)__/g, (match, index)=>{

export const fetchQuestions = async (mode, topicName, userData, subjectContext)=>{
    const isPremium = userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.isSubscribed;
    let masteredCount = 0;
    if ("object" !== "undefined") {
        masteredCount = getMasteredQuestions().length;
    }
    const safeId = getTestBankId(mode, topicName, userData, subjectContext) + "_v4_m" + masteredCount;
    const fullTopic = subjectContext ? "".concat(subjectContext, " - ").concat(topicName) : topicName;
    const qRef = doc(db, "global_questions", safeId);
    try {
        let rawData = null;
        let mistakes = [];
        let mastered = [];
        if ("object" !== "undefined") {
            const allMistakes = getMistakes();
            mistakes = allMistakes.filter((m)=>m.topicName === topicName || m.subject === topicName || fullTopic.includes(m.subject)).slice(0, 5);
            mastered = getMasteredQuestions();
        }
        const numNeeded = mode === "mock50" ? 50 : Math.max(10 - mistakes.length, 1);
        let adaptiveContext = subjectContext || "";
        if (mastered.length > 0) {
            adaptiveContext += "\n\n\uD83D\uDD34 ADAPTIVE RULE: DO NOT generate questions similar to these (Student already mastered them): ".concat(mastered.slice(-15).join(" | "));
        }
        adaptiveContext += "\n\n\uD83C\uDFAF GENERATE EXACTLY ".concat(numNeeded, " QUESTIONS.");
        rawData = await generateAIQuestions(fullTopic, userData, adaptiveContext, numNeeded.toString());
        if (mistakes.length > 0 && mode !== "mock50") {
            const recycledQs = mistakes.map((m)=>{
                const mOptions = Array.isArray(m.options) ? m.options : m.options ? [
                    m.options
                ] : [
                    "A",
                    "B",
                    "C",
                    "D"
                ];
                let cIndex = 0;
                if (typeof m.correctAnswer === "number") {
                    cIndex = m.correctAnswer;
                } else if (typeof m.correctAnswer === "string") {
                    cIndex = mOptions.findIndex((opt)=>typeof opt === "string" && opt.trim().toLowerCase() === m.correctAnswer.trim().toLowerCase());
                    if (cIndex === -1) cIndex = 0;
                }
                return {
                    text: m.question || m.text || "Previously missed question",
                    options: mOptions,
                    correct: cIndex,
                    explanation: "Let's try this again! You made a mistake on this previously.\n\n" + (m.explanation || ""),
                    difficulty: "Medium",
                    importance: "High"
                };
            });
            rawData = [
                ...recycledQs,
                ...rawData
            ];
        }
        rawData = rawData.slice(0, mode === "mock50" ? 50 : 10);
        rawData.sort(()=>Math.random() - 0.5);
        if (!rawData || rawData.length === 0) throw new Error("Empty questions");
        try {
            await setDoc(qRef, {
                questions: rawData,
                createdAt: serverTimestamp()
            });
        } catch (e) {
            console.warn("Failed to cache questions:", e);
        }
        const mapped = rawData.map((q)=>{
            const resolvedCorrect = q.correctAnswer !== undefined ? q.correctAnswer : q.correct !== undefined ? q.correct : 0;
            return {
                ...q,
                correctAnswer: resolvedCorrect,
                correct: resolvedCorrect
            };
        });
        let corrected = autoCorrectMCQs(mapped);
        return corrected;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Error fetching questions:", error);
        return [];
    }
};
export const fetchDoubtResponse = async function(question) {
    let context = arguments.length > 1 && arguments[1] !== void 0 ? arguments[1] : "";
    try {
        const { model } = await import("./gemini");
        const prompt = "You are an expert Indian school teacher. Answer this student's doubt clearly and concisely in 3-5 lines, using simple language and examples. Question: \"".concat(question, '"');
        const result = await model.generateContent(prompt);
        return result.response.text();
    } catch (e) {
        return "AI Teacher is currently busy. Please try again in a moment.";
    }
};

        "Science",

export const fetchContent = async function(mode) {
    let parentId = arguments.length > 1 && arguments[1] !== void 0 ? arguments[1] : null, type = arguments.length > 2 ? arguments[2] : void 0;
    // Check localStorage cache first for instant load
    const cached = getCachedContent(mode, parentId, type);
    if (cached && Array.isArray(cached) && cached.length > 0) {
        return cached;
    }
    const extract = (prefix)=>{
        if (!parentId) return null;
        const match = parentId.match(new RegExp("".concat(prefix, "_(.*?)(?=__categories_|__exams_|__years_|__boards_|__classes_|__subjects_|__chapters_|__topics_|$)"), "i"));
        return match ? match[1] : null;
    };
    let list = [];
    if (type === "Categories") {
        list = [
            "School",
            "Competitive"
        ];
    } else if (type === "Boards") {
        list = INDIAN_BOARDS;
    } else if (type === "Classes") {
        list = CLASSES;
    } else if (type === "Subjects") {
        // Convert raw extracted values to proper format before lookup
        const clsRaw = extract("classes") || "class_10";
        const boardRaw = extract("boards") || "cbse";
        // class_10 -> "Class 10", class_12 -> "Class 12"
        const cls = clsRaw.startsWith("class_") ? "Class ".concat(clsRaw.replace("class_", "")) : clsRaw.includes("Class") ? clsRaw : "Class ".concat(clsRaw);
        // cbse -> "CBSE", match against INDIAN_BOARDS list
        const boardNormalized = boardRaw.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_");
        const board = INDIAN_BOARDS.find((b)=>b.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_").startsWith(boardNormalized)) || boardRaw.toUpperCase();
        list = getSubjects(cls, board);
    } else if (type === "Chapters") {
        const classRaw = extract("classes");
        const subRaw = extract("subjects");
        const boardRaw = extract("boards");
        const cls = classRaw ? classRaw.startsWith("class_") ? "Class ".concat(classRaw.replace("class_", "")) : "Class ".concat(classRaw) : "Class 10";
        const sub = subRaw ? subRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : "Science";
        const board = boardRaw ? INDIAN_BOARDS.find((b)=>b.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_") === boardRaw) || "" : "";
        const staticChapters = getChapters(sub, cls, board);
        if (staticChapters && staticChapters.length > 0) {
            list = staticChapters;
        } else {
            const discoveryId = "chapters_".concat(board, "_").concat(cls, "_").concat(sub, "_v3").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "_");
            const docRef = doc(db, "global_chapters", discoveryId);
            try {
                let snap = null;
                try {
                    snap = await getDoc(docRef);
                } catch (dbErr) {
                    console.warn("Failed to read global_chapters:", dbErr);
                }
                if (snap && snap.exists()) {
                    list = snap.data().chapters;
                } else {
                    list = await generateAIChapters(board, cls, sub);
                    if (list && list.length > 0) {
                        try {
                            await setDoc(docRef, {
                                chapters: list,
                                createdAt: serverTimestamp()
                            });
                        } catch (e) {
                            console.warn("Failed to cache chapters", e);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                list = [
                    "Chapter 1",
                    "Chapter 2"
                ];
            }
        }
    } else if (type === "Topics") {
        const classRaw = extract("classes");
        const subRaw = extract("subjects");
        const boardRaw = extract("boards");
        const chapterRaw = extract("chapters");
        const cls = classRaw ? classRaw.startsWith("class_") ? "Class ".concat(classRaw.replace("class_", "")) : "Class ".concat(classRaw) : "Class 10";
        const sub = subRaw ? subRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : "Science";
        const board = boardRaw ? INDIAN_BOARDS.find((b)=>b.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_") === boardRaw) || "" : "";
        const chapter = chapterRaw ? chapterRaw.replace(/_/g, " ") : "Chapter 1";
        const staticTopics = getTopics(chapter, sub, cls);
        if (staticTopics && staticTopics.length > 0) {
            list = staticTopics;
        } else {
            const discoveryId = "topics_".concat(board, "_").concat(cls, "_").concat(sub, "_").concat(chapter, "_v3").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "_");
            const docRef = doc(db, "global_topics", discoveryId);
            try {
                let snap = null;
                try {
                    snap = await getDoc(docRef);
                } catch (dbErr) {
                    console.warn("Failed to read global_topics:", dbErr);
                }
                if (snap && snap.exists()) {
                    list = snap.data().topics;
                } else {
                    list = await generateAISyllabus(board, cls, sub, chapter);
                    if (list && list.length > 0) {
                        try {
                            await setDoc(docRef, {
                                topics: list,
                                createdAt: serverTimestamp()
                            });
                        } catch (e) {
                            console.warn("Failed to cache topics", e);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                list = [
                    "Topic 1",
                    "Topic 2"
                ];
            }
        }
    }
    if (!list) list = [];
    const result = list.map((item)=>({
            id: "".concat(parentId ? parentId + "__" : "").concat(type.toLowerCase(), "_").concat(item.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_")),
            name: item,
            type: type === "Boards" ? "classes" : type === "Classes" ? "subjects" : type === "Subjects" ? "chapters" : type === "Chapters" ? "topics" : type === "Topics" ? "subtopics" : "leaf",
            parentId
        }));
    if (result && result.length > 0) {
        saveContentToCache(mode, parentId, type, result);
    }
    return result;
};
export const analyzePerformance = async (userId, history)=>{
    try {
        const data = await generateAIAnalysis({
            id: userId,
            history
        });
        return data;
    } catch (error) {
        return {
            weakAreas: [
                "General Revision Required"
            ],
            tips: "Consistent practice will help."
        };
    }
};

    if (false) {}

const getCachedContent = (mode, parentId, type)=>{
    if (false) {}
    const key = "achivox_".concat(mode, "_").concat(parentId || "root", "_").concat(type, "_").concat(achivox_cache_version);
    const data = localStorage.getItem(key);

const getTestBankId = (mode, topicName, userData, subjectContext)=>{

            subjectiveQuestions: (rawData.subjectiveQuestions || ((_rawData_questions = rawData.questions) === null || _rawData_questions === void 0 ? void 0 : _rawData_questions.subjective) || []).map((q)=>({
                    q: q.q || q.question || "",
                    a: q.a || q.answer || "",
                    easyWay: q.easyWay || q.tip || q.shortcut || "",
                    weightage: q.weightage || q.marks || (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 5 : 3)
                })),
            objectiveQuestions: rawData.objectiveQuestions || ((_rawData_questions1 = rawData.questions) === null || _rawData_questions1 === void 0 ? void 0 : _rawData_questions1.objective) || []
        };
        // Safely attempt to write cache, but catch any database restriction errors
        try {
            await setDoc(noteRef, {
                ...compatibleData,
                createdAt: serverTimestamp()
            });
        } catch (dbErr) {
            console.warn("Failed to cache global_notes in Firestore:", dbErr);
        }
        return compatibleData;
    } catch (e) {
        console.error("fetchChapterNotes error:", e);
        await logToTerminal("fetchChapterNotes ERROR for ".concat(topicName, ": ").concat(e.message), "error");
        return null;
    }
};

export const getTestBankId = (mode, topicName, userData, subjectContext)=>{
    const boardKey = (userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.board) || "CBSE";
    const classKey = (userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.cls) || "10th";
    const fullTopic = subjectContext ? "".concat(subjectContext, " - ").concat(topicName) : topicName;
    return "questions_".concat(mode, "_").concat(boardKey, "_").concat(classKey, "_").concat(fullTopic, "_").concat(achivox_cache_version).replace(/[\/\.#$\[\]\s]/g, "_").toLowerCase();
};
export const fetchQuestions = async (mode, topicName, userData, subjectContext)=>{
    const isPremium = userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.isSubscribed;
    let masteredCount = 0;
    if ("object" !== "undefined") {
        masteredCount = getMasteredQuestions().length;
    }
    const safeId = getTestBankId(mode, topicName, userData, subjectContext) + "_v4_m" + masteredCount;
    const fullTopic = subjectContext ? "".concat(subjectContext, " - ").concat(topicName) : topicName;
    const qRef = doc(db, "global_questions", safeId);
    try {
        let rawData = null;
        let mistakes = [];
        let mastered = [];
        if ("object" !== "undefined") {
            const allMistakes = getMistakes();
            mistakes = allMistakes.filter((m)=>m.topicName === topicName || m.subject === topicName || fullTopic.includes(m.subject)).slice(0, 5);
            mastered = getMasteredQuestions();
        }
        const numNeeded = mode === "mock50" ? 50 : Math.max(10 - mistakes.length, 1);
        let adaptiveContext = subjectContext || "";
        if (mastered.length > 0) {
            adaptiveContext += "\n\n\uD83D\uDD34 ADAPTIVE RULE: DO NOT generate questions similar to these (Student already mastered them): ".concat(mastered.slice(-15).join(" | "));
        }
        adaptiveContext += "\n\n\uD83C\uDFAF GENERATE EXACTLY ".concat(numNeeded, " QUESTIONS.");
        rawData = await generateAIQuestions(fullTopic, userData, adaptiveContext, numNeeded.toString());
        if (mistakes.length > 0 && mode !== "mock50") {
            const recycledQs = mistakes.map((m)=>{
                const mOptions = Array.isArray(m.options) ? m.options : m.options ? [
                    m.options
                ] : [
                    "A",
                    "B",
                    "C",
                    "D"
                ];
                let cIndex = 0;
                if (typeof m.correctAnswer === "number") {
                    cIndex = m.correctAnswer;
                } else if (typeof m.correctAnswer === "string") {
                    cIndex = mOptions.findIndex((opt)=>typeof opt === "string" && opt.trim().toLowerCase() === m.correctAnswer.trim().toLowerCase());
                    if (cIndex === -1) cIndex = 0;
                }
                return {
                    text: m.question || m.text || "Previously missed question",
                    options: mOptions,
                    correct: cIndex,
                    explanation: "Let's try this again! You made a mistake on this previously.\n\n" + (m.explanation || ""),
                    difficulty: "Medium",
                    importance: "High"
                };
            });
            rawData = [
                ...recycledQs,
                ...rawData
            ];
        }
        rawData = rawData.slice(0, mode === "mock50" ? 50 : 10);
        rawData.sort(()=>Math.random() - 0.5);
        if (!rawData || rawData.length === 0) throw new Error("Empty questions");
        try {
            await setDoc(qRef, {
                questions: rawData,
                createdAt: serverTimestamp()
            });
        } catch (e) {
            console.warn("Failed to cache questions:", e);
        }
        const mapped = rawData.map((q)=>{
            const resolvedCorrect = q.correctAnswer !== undefined ? q.correctAnswer : q.correct !== undefined ? q.correct : 0;
            return {
                ...q,
                correctAnswer: resolvedCorrect,
                correct: resolvedCorrect
            };
        });
        let corrected = autoCorrectMCQs(mapped);
        return corrected;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Error fetching questions:", error);
        return [];
    }
};
export const fetchDoubtResponse = async function(question) {
    let context = arguments.length > 1 && arguments[1] !== void 0 ? arguments[1] : "";
    try {
        const { model } = await import("./gemini");
        const prompt = "You are an expert Indian school teacher. Answer this student's doubt clearly and concisely in 3-5 lines, using simple language and examples. Question: \"".concat(question, '"');
        const result = await model.generateContent(prompt);
        return result.response.text();
    } catch (e) {
        return "AI Teacher is currently busy. Please try again in a moment.";
    }
};

        "Science",
        "Maths"
    ];

export const fetchContent = async function(mode) {
    let parentId = arguments.length > 1 && arguments[1] !== void 0 ? arguments[1] : null, type = arguments.length > 2 ? arguments[2] : void 0;
    // Check localStorage cache first for instant load
    const cached = getCachedContent(mode, parentId, type);
    if (cached && Array.isArray(cached) && cached.length > 0) {
        return cached;
    }
    const extract = (prefix)=>{
        if (!parentId) return null;
        const match = parentId.match(new RegExp("".concat(prefix, "_(.*?)(?=__categories_|__exams_|__years_|__boards_|__classes_|__subjects_|__chapters_|__topics_|$)"), "i"));
        return match ? match[1] : null;
    };
    let list = [];
    if (type === "Categories") {
        list = [
            "School",
            "Competitive"
        ];
    } else if (type === "Boards") {
        list = INDIAN_BOARDS;
    } else if (type === "Classes") {
        list = CLASSES;
    } else if (type === "Subjects") {
        // Convert raw extracted values to proper format before lookup
        const clsRaw = extract("classes") || "class_10";
        const boardRaw = extract("boards") || "cbse";
        // class_10 -> "Class 10", class_12 -> "Class 12"
        const cls = clsRaw.startsWith("class_") ? "Class ".concat(clsRaw.replace("class_", "")) : clsRaw.includes("Class") ? clsRaw : "Class ".concat(clsRaw);
        // cbse -> "CBSE", match against INDIAN_BOARDS list
        const boardNormalized = boardRaw.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_");
        const board = INDIAN_BOARDS.find((b)=>b.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_").startsWith(boardNormalized)) || boardRaw.toUpperCase();
        list = getSubjects(cls, board);
    } else if (type === "Chapters") {
        const classRaw = extract("classes");
        const subRaw = extract("subjects");
        const boardRaw = extract("boards");
        const cls = classRaw ? classRaw.startsWith("class_") ? "Class ".concat(classRaw.replace("class_", "")) : "Class ".concat(classRaw) : "Class 10";
        const sub = subRaw ? subRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : "Science";
        const board = boardRaw ? INDIAN_BOARDS.find((b)=>b.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_") === boardRaw) || "" : "";
        const staticChapters = getChapters(sub, cls, board);
        if (staticChapters && staticChapters.length > 0) {
            list = staticChapters;
        } else {
            const discoveryId = "chapters_".concat(board, "_").concat(cls, "_").concat(sub, "_v3").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "_");
            const docRef = doc(db, "global_chapters", discoveryId);
            try {
                let snap = null;
                try {
                    snap = await getDoc(docRef);
                } catch (dbErr) {
                    console.warn("Failed to read global_chapters:", dbErr);
                }
                if (snap && snap.exists()) {
                    list = snap.data().chapters;
                } else {
                    list = await generateAIChapters(board, cls, sub);
                    if (list && list.length > 0) {
                        try {
                            await setDoc(docRef, {
                                chapters: list,
                                createdAt: serverTimestamp()
                            });
                        } catch (e) {
                            console.warn("Failed to cache chapters", e);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                list = [
                    "Chapter 1",
                    "Chapter 2"
                ];
            }
        }
    } else if (type === "Topics") {
        const classRaw = extract("classes");
        const subRaw = extract("subjects");
        const boardRaw = extract("boards");
        const chapterRaw = extract("chapters");
        const cls = classRaw ? classRaw.startsWith("class_") ? "Class ".concat(classRaw.replace("class_", "")) : "Class ".concat(classRaw) : "Class 10";
        const sub = subRaw ? subRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : "Science";
        const board = boardRaw ? INDIAN_BOARDS.find((b)=>b.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_") === boardRaw) || "" : "";
        const chapter = chapterRaw ? chapterRaw.replace(/_/g, " ") : "Chapter 1";
        const staticTopics = getTopics(chapter, sub, cls);
        if (staticTopics && staticTopics.length > 0) {
            list = staticTopics;
        } else {
            const discoveryId = "topics_".concat(board, "_").concat(cls, "_").concat(sub, "_").concat(chapter, "_v3").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "_");
            const docRef = doc(db, "global_topics", discoveryId);
            try {
                let snap = null;
                try {
                    snap = await getDoc(docRef);
                } catch (dbErr) {
                    console.warn("Failed to read global_topics:", dbErr);
                }
                if (snap && snap.exists()) {
                    list = snap.data().topics;
                } else {
                    list = await generateAISyllabus(board, cls, sub, chapter);
                    if (list && list.length > 0) {
                        try {
                            await setDoc(docRef, {
                                topics: list,
                                createdAt: serverTimestamp()
                            });
                        } catch (e) {
                            console.warn("Failed to cache topics", e);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                list = [
                    "Topic 1",
                    "Topic 2"
                ];
            }
        }
    }
    if (!list) list = [];
    const result = list.map((item)=>({
            id: "".concat(parentId ? parentId + "__" : "").concat(type.toLowerCase(), "_").concat(item.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "_")),
            name: item,
            type: type === "Boards" ? "classes" : type === "Classes" ? "subjects" : type === "Subjects" ? "chapters" : type === "Chapters" ? "topics" : type === "Topics" ? "subtopics" : "leaf",
            parentId
        }));
    if (result && result.length > 0) {
        saveContentToCache(mode, parentId, type, result);
    }
    return result;
};

                    const requiredDays = isPremium ? 7 : 30;

                    }

const fetchQuestions = async (mode, topicName, userData, subjectContext)=>{
    const isPremium = userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.isSubscribed;
    let masteredCount = 0;
    if (true) {
        masteredCount = (0,_analytics__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_3__/* .getMasteredQuestions */ .eD)().length;
    }
    const safeId = getTestBankId(mode, topicName, userData, subjectContext) + "_v4_m" + masteredCount;
    const fullTopic = subjectContext ? "".concat(subjectContext, " - ").concat(topicName) : topicName;
    const qRef = (0,firebase_firestore__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_1__/* .doc */ .JU)(_firebase__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_0__.db, "global_questions", safeId);
    try {
        let rawData = null;
        let mistakes = [];
        let mastered = [];
        if (true) {
            const allMistakes = (0,_analytics__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_3__/* .getMistakes */ .Yj)();
            mistakes = allMistakes.filter((m)=>m.topicName === topicName || m.subject === topicName || fullTopic.includes(m.subject)).slice(0, 5);
            mastered = (0,_analytics__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_3__/* .getMasteredQuestions */ .eD)();
        }
        const numNeeded = mode === "mock50" ? 50 : Math.max(10 - mistakes.length, 1);
        let adaptiveContext = subjectContext || "";
        if (mastered.length > 0) {
            adaptiveContext += "\n\n\uD83D\uDD34 ADAPTIVE RULE: DO NOT generate questions similar to these (Student already mastered them): ".concat(mastered.slice(-15).join(" | "));
        }
        adaptiveContext += "\n\n\uD83C\uDFAF GENERATE EXACTLY ".concat(numNeeded, " QUESTIONS.");
        rawData = await (0,_gemini__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_2__/* .generateAIQuestions */ .Fk)(fullTopic, userData, adaptiveContext, numNeeded.toString());
        if (mistakes.length > 0 && mode !== "mock50") {
            const recycledQs = mistakes.map((m)=>{
                const mOptions = Array.isArray(m.options) ? m.options : m.options ? [
                    m.options
                ] : [
                    "A",
                    "B",
                    "C",
                    "D"
                ];
                let cIndex = 0;
                if (typeof m.correctAnswer === "number") {
                    cIndex = m.correctAnswer;
                } else if (typeof m.correctAnswer === "string") {
                    cIndex = mOptions.findIndex((opt)=>typeof opt === "string" && opt.trim().toLowerCase() === m.correctAnswer.trim().toLowerCase());
                    if (cIndex === -1) cIndex = 0;
                }
                return {
                    text: m.question || m.text || "Previously missed question",
                    options: mOptions,
                    correct: cIndex,
                    explanation: "Let's try this again! You made a mistake on this previously.\n\n" + (m.explanation || ""),
                    difficulty: "Medium",
                    importance: "High"
                };
            });
            rawData = [
                ...recycledQs,
                ...rawData
            ];
        }
        rawData = rawData.slice(0, mode === "mock50" ? 50 : 10);
        rawData.sort(()=>Math.random() - 0.5);
        if (!rawData || rawData.length === 0) throw new Error("Empty questions");
        try {
            await (0,firebase_firestore__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_1__/* .setDoc */ .pl)(qRef, {
                questions: rawData,
                createdAt: (0,firebase_firestore__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_1__/* .serverTimestamp */ .Bt)()
            });
        } catch (e) {
            console.warn("Failed to cache questions:", e);
        }
        const mapped = rawData.map((q)=>{
            const resolvedCorrect = q.correctAnswer !== undefined ? q.correctAnswer : q.correct !== undefined ? q.correct : 0;
            return {
                ...q,
                correctAnswer: resolvedCorrect,
                correct: resolvedCorrect
            };
        });
        let corrected = (0,_gemini__WEBPACK_IMPORTED_MODULE_2__/* .autoCorrectMCQs */ .y7)(mapped);
        return corrected;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Error fetching questions:", error);
        return [];
    }
};
const fetchDoubtResponse = async function(question) {
